    /*Disable Omniture Tracking*/
 
 
 
 var s = {};
 
 
 
 s.t = s.tl  = function(){};
 
 
 
 var s_gi = function(){return s;};
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 /*Global Modules*/
 
 
 
 function getQueryString() {
 
 
 
         var querystring = new Array;
 
 
 
         var q = String(document.location).split("?")[1];
 
 
 
         if (!q) {
 
 
 
             return false
 
 
 
         }
 
 
 
         q = q.split("&");
 
 
 
         for (var i = 0; i < q.length; i++) {
 
 
 
             var o = q[i].split("=");
 
 
 
             querystring[o[0]] = o[1]
 
 
 
         }
 
 
 
         return querystring
 
 
 
     }
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
     function getHashString() {
 
 
 
         var qs = new Array;
 
 
 
         var q = String(document.location).split("#")[1];
 
 
 
         if (!q) {
 
 
 
             return false
 
 
 
         }
 
 
 
         q = q.split("&");
 
 
 
         for (var i = 0; i < q.length; i++) {
 
 
 
             var o = q[i].split("=");
 
 
 
             qs[o[0]] = o[1]
 
 
 
         }
 
 
 
         return qs
 
 
 
     }

      $().ready(function() {

             var $exitMsgLink = $('#exit_msg > a');
             var $somaLink = $('#menu_soma > a');
             var divHeight = $exitMsg.height();
             $exitMsg.hide().css({ height : 0 });
             $somaLink.click(function(){
                 $exitMsg.animate({ height : divHeight, opacity: .9}, 1000);
             });
             $somaLink.mouseout(function() {
                 $somaLink.oneTime(1000, 'hide', function() {
                     $exitMsg.animate({ height: 0 }, 500,  function () {
                         $exitMsg.hide();
                     });
                 });
             });

                 $somaLink.stopTime('hide');
